<review>Wow, where do I begin?

This easily has to be some of the worst service I've had to work with. I work for a collision shop and had to order a set of wheels for a customer through this tire shop as it was where the customer had originally gotten their wheels.

Well, the wheels we needed were discontinued, which is not their fault. And they did initially help me get a couple different options for our customer to choose from. We decided on a new style, got them special ordered in the same size for all 4 wheels because the car was AWD (this is important later on) and waited for the shipping. They told me about 3-4 business days, no problem.

And here is where the issues begin. As we start to pull apart the old wheels and tires so we could re-use the good tires, we notice something strange. The wheels that were on the car were two different sizes in width! Even though the tires were the same size all around. Now, these wheels are meant to be a replica of some Mercedes wheels that are for a RWD car, which in that case staggering the wheel size like that is okay. However on an AWD drive car this is NOT okay. Putting different sizes of wheels on an AWD car can severely damage the transmission and differentials. Not to mention that since the tires were all the same size, 2 of them were being stretch fit, which is unsafe.

But hey, whatever, we're fixing that with putting 4 same size wheels on.

Now cut to when the wheels were supposed to have arrived. I call them asking where the wheels are, and they say they haven't shown up, they'll be in tomorrow. Okay, no biggie. Tomorrow comes, i call again and the wheels are in! Awesome, they say they'll deliver them that day.

Welp, it's nearly the end of the day and still no wheels. I call in to ask what's up and I get told that actually our wheels are not in. But wait, I was told that they were in just that morning right? Apparently not.

This happens multiple times over the course of multiple days. The customer, Estimator, and I are getting increasingly upset aout how this situation is being handled.

But finally! After nearly 10 business days we get our wheels, get them mounted and get the customer on their way...or so we thought. We get a call back that a little AMG sticker that goes on the wheel (which was in the photo we were sent by them to show our customer) isn't on the wheel. We never received them so I call again.

Person at Bayfair says they don't usually send them out but she'll throw them in an envelope and mail them to us no problem.....It's now been a month and still no AMG sticker. I've called 3 times today and apparently no one there is willing to help. What a joke.

I cannot recommend this shop to anyone because the service I received was an absolute joke and extremely dismissive.<//review>< pics>

< Review>
Dr Pechak is an absolute master, skilled beyond belief, with decades of experience and the very latest techniques.  READ THIS + SEE PHOTOS IF YOU HAVE GUM RECESSION AND WILL GRAFT OR PINHOLE!! He is by far one of the very best doctors I have ever experienced. I should start by saying I am very fussy and particular.  I have a moderate pain tolerance, I suffer from anxiety before a treatment and research well before I take the chance on any new doctor. I went to him with severe recession and I specifically wanted to have pinhole technique. I had already had traditional graft once before on one-side and was unhappy, having had an extremely difficult recovery. I pinned my hopes on him and he delivered what I wanted, but rightfully outlined that I needed the traditional grafting method on the top and was eligible for pinhole on the bottom. He made a plan to treat both sides of my mouth, in two stages, over 5 months apart.

I am now 5 days post my second surgery in writing and I could not be happier. He is straightforward, direct and honest. He photographs everything, walks you through and explains everything and puts you at ease.  It was important for me to write this after the second surgery so I could test the consistency and the recovery.

Unlike other doctors, he does not cut and stitch the palette (which is a nightmare). Instead, he makes a precise, very small incision on the side that the tissue is being grafted from in roof and then places a plastic mouth guard over the entire roof (made to measure) ‚Äì not one suture in roof! This plastic guard sits there for 24 hours after surgery. You simply pop it off 24 hours later, and you are healed. To expedite this, they take blood and centrifuge it and add it to the wound during surgery. You will not believe how quickly you heal. After 24 hours, you can go about your business. Even drinking and eating=zero irritation. Anywhere else, lives in the past and is dated if they do not do it like this when the tech is available!!

The pinhole is equally amazing. He adds stitches to the pinhole surgery, so there is a small modification to the Chao technique ‚Äì which I love! This is even easier than the traditional graft ‚Äì just collagen filled in through a small hole. Very little pain or discomfort.  The sutures help to keep it in place and I have achieved results that are fantastic! If you qualify for this, have it done!! Dr Pechak will assess as needed.

I have the traditional graft + pinhole done in one session (having now had it done twice). Both times, the consistency of the surgery was amazing. I have healed beautifully, I was back to work after a couple of days of rest, and I had controlled swelling.  The instructions are clear and concise.

Finally, Dr Pechak and his entire staff care ‚Äì deeply ‚Äì  that you have good results, you heal, you feel happy and are comfortable. I consider them to be caregivers, not just a doctors office. Clarissa who deals with your insurance is unbelievable at her job ‚Äì she is diligent, kind, caring, makes sure all your paperwork is in order and explains everything like a pro. She is fantastic and has been a rock for me through the process. Nidhi who runs the front desk is again so sweet, kind and attentive to your needs. When you arrive, they greet you so warmly ‚Äì it  makes all the difference to have them hold your hand through this process! You realize that its not just about the doctor but their entire team. Nurses, equally fantastic and chat with you, talk you through everything and settle you in nicely.
I attach three photos for you to see:
1. Right - Shows the right side healing 5 days after surgery
2. Left - Shows left side after 5 months
3. Shows Left side 5 days after surgery
The ones after 5 days are early in healing, showing you how much coverage was achieved,  how it settles and heals 5 months down the line!</Review>

<UserId.>106664542778851377241</UserId.><user_name>cilla wright<//user_name><date>1522301917616</date><Rating>5< /Rating>< Text>
Dr Pechak is an absolute master, skilled beyond belief, with decades of experience and the very latest techniques.  READ THIS + SEE PHOTOS IF YOU HAVE GUM RECESSION AND WILL GRAFT OR PINHOLE!! I would not hesitate, there is no-one better in U.S, forget Silicon Valley. I have just completed my 5mo x2 procedures for gum graft.  I consider offices that do not follow his state-of-the-art techniques to be living in the past.

He is by far one of the very best doctors I have ever experienced. I should start by saying I am very fussy and particular.  I have a moderate pain tolerance, I suffer from anxiety before a treatment and research well before I take the chance on any new doctor. I went to him with severe recession and I specifically wanted to have pinhole technique. I had already had traditional graft once before on one-side and was unhappy, having had an extremely difficult recovery. I pinned my hopes on him and he delivered what I wanted, but rightfully outlined that I needed the traditional grafting method on the top and was eligible for pinhole on the bottom. He made a plan to treat both sides of my mouth, in two stages, over 5 months apart.

I am now 5 days post my second surgery in writing and I could not be happier. He is straightforward, direct and honest. He photographs everything, walks you through and explains everything and puts you at ease.  It was important for me to write this after the second surgery so I could test the consistency and the recovery.

Unlike other doctors, he does not cut and stitch the palette (which is a nightmare). Instead, he makes a precise, very small incision on the side that the tissue is being grafted from in roof and then places a plastic mouth guard over the entire roof (made to measure) ‚Äì not one suture in roof! This plastic guard sits there for 24 hours after surgery. You simply pop it off 24 hours later, and you are healed. To expedite this, they take blood and centrifuge it and add it to the wound during surgery. You will not believe how quickly you heal. After 24 hours, you can go about your business. Even drinking and eating=zero irritation. Anywhere else, lives in the past and is dated if they do not do it like this when the tech is available!!

The pinhole is equally amazing. He adds stitches to the pinhole surgery, so there is a small modification to the Chao technique ‚Äì which I love! This is even easier than the traditional graft ‚Äì just collagen filled in through a small hole. Very little pain or discomfort.  The sutures help to keep it in place and I have achieved results that are fantastic! If you qualify for this, have it done!! Dr Pechak will assess as needed.

I have the traditional graft + pinhole done in one session (having now had it done twice). Both times, the consistency of the surgery was amazing. I have healed beautifully, I was back to work after a couple of days of rest, and I had controlled swelling.  The instructions are clear and concise.

Finally, Dr Pechak and his entire staff care ‚Äì deeply ‚Äì  that you have good results, you heal, you feel happy and are comfortable. I consider them to be caregivers, not just a doctors office. Clarissa who deals with your insurance is unbelievable at her job ‚Äì she is diligent, kind, caring, makes sure all your paperwork is in order and explains everything like a pro. She is fantastic and has been a rock for me through the process. Nidhi who runs the front desk is again so sweet, kind and attentive to your needs. When you arrive, they greet you so warmly ‚Äì it  makes all the difference to have them hold your hand through this process! You realize that its not just about the doctor but their entire team. Nurses, equally fantastic and chat with you, talk you through everything and settle you in nicely.
I attach three photos for you to see:
1. Right - Shows the right side healing 5 days after surgery
2. Left - Shows left side after 5 months
3. Shows Left side 5 days after surgery
The ones after 5 days are early in healing, showing you how much coverage was achieved,  how it settles and heals 5 months down the line!<//Text>

< Text>
Dr. Pechak and his team are fantastic - truly first class service with an exceptional outcome.  I initially came in for a second opinion after my original periodontist had proposed expensive and painful traditional periodontal flap surgery on all four quadrants.  Dr. Pechak's recommendation that I would be an ideal candidate for LANAP surgery almost sounded too good to be true, as the procedure had minimal recovery time and actually came in cheaper than the traditional surgical approach.  However, 6 months later and the procedure was a resounding success, reducing pockets depths that were up 2 7, 8 and even 9mm, to healthy 2-3mm pockets, with very healthy surrounding gum tissue.

Throughout the preparation, procedure, and post-surgical check-ins, Dr. Pechak and his team were careful to answer all my questions to set my concerns at ease, and were incredibly professional throughout.  I had been putting this procedure off for years because of fears and concerns about the post-operative discomfort, and Dr. Pechak's approach using LANAP couldn't have been easier or gone better.

I would confidently recommend him for your first (and probably only) opinion if you are looking for a dentist proficient in cutting edge, highly effective approaches to treating any serious periodontal issues you are dealing with.< /Text>

<Review>No one likes hearing that they need to have a tooth removed, and replaced with an implant. But, if you have to hear that you want to be sitting in the exam chair at Doctor Pechak office.  There is no one better in the Bay Area.

My molar had a cracked root and had to come out. It was extracted under local anesthetic in under an hour. Dr. Pechak uses state of the art equipment and advanced techniques to assure great results.

For example, Dr. Pechak uses your own healing factors from a small amount of blood he draws before the procedure. In blood plasma are palettes and other good things that make us heal. By mixing those with tiny pieces of bone and inserting that in the hole where the tooth used to be healing occurs quicker and with less chance of complications.

The proof is, I left the office with a regime of antibiotics and Motrin. I never needed more that. I had no post-surgery bleeding or pain. By the second day I was eating everything I normally do, I just had to chew on the other side of my mouth.

Dr Pechak is a perfectionist. That isn‚Äôt a good trait for a Barista making your daily latte, but it‚Äôs great when it comes to having your teeth and mouth work properly and stay healthy. There isn‚Äôt anybody I would trust more than Dr. Pechak to do that for me.

Face it, oral surgery is a big inconvenience and very costly, and in the Bay Area there are few bargains. Since you already know that you might as well choose someone who is going do the procedure in the most effective and painless way and produce great results.

My Mom used to say: be true to your teeth or they will be false to you, and my Dad used to say: pay for the best and cry only once.< /Review>< pics>

< Review>
I have been seeing Teri Drew for over a year now, I have been treated with respect from the first day from both the staff and clinicians. I was initially asked by my doctor to come here for psychiatric meds as it is very tough for a medical doctor to prescribe these now that the opiod epidemic has started :( I sort of came begrudgingly, but since my health insurance was willing to foot the cost (except for a $40 copay) I decided I would go and make things easier for my doctor. I am so happy I made the decision to come in, not only have I experienced great advise and counseling, Teri has really helped me (partnered with me) to make the best decisions I can make regarding medication and life decisions, she is very knowledgeable with meds, side effects and what works with what. I can honestly state that this is the best I have felt (I am 55), my depression is non-existent, my anxieties are manageable now and my sleep cycles are returning. Teri was not forceful with her advise which helped me excel, I think she knows when you need a little push and will give that if needed, but mostly I feel this is a partnership allowing me to feel the best I can about my life! I want to state again, I have had nothing but positive attitudes from everyone I have met at Siyan and appreciate everyone from the front desk staff, to my doctor, to the doctor that filled in for her and helped me with my meds while she was away on vacation...I would definitely suggest this business to anyone that has the need! :)
I have met now with one of the other clinicians and she is terrific as well! They are doing tele visits now and that is very helpful during Covid, though their office is immaculate and they have loads of Covid protections in place.
I am also now meeting with Carrie and she is also wonderful and has many good ideas on how to curb anger and depression. I will continue to work with her on these items and many more. The staff at Siyan are all wonderful, very wonderful and helpful!< /Review>

Update (as of 09/17):
Gina was able to reach out to me today, and I finally felt that my concerns were finally addressed. When she first called me and identified herself from RSM Ford, I have to admit that I was initially annoyed and defensive during our conversation.

However, during that call she allowed me to gain her trust and I was able to express my experiences (the 3 visits so far). I felt that she understood my concerns and she's an excellent active listener.

I mentioned that I have nothing personal against the Service Advisor who (tried to) assisted me, however the customer experience I went through can be greatly improved.

At first, I decided to go have my SUV serviced at RSM Ford due to the convenience factor; it's nice to know that if I wanted to make an appointment, it can literally be done same day (which is kind of unheard of when it comes to other dealerships)!

After talking with Gina to finally air things out, I now do not think discrimination took place; it was just a misunderstanding with the Service Advisor who unknowingly didn't know how to de-escalate situations.

Gina has restored my faith in this dealership, and I may give them another chance during my next service visit. If this momentum continues, I may seriously consider SM Ford for my next vehicle purchase (hopefully the new Bronco within the next 2 years).

Because of Gina, I'm updating their rating from 1 to 4 stars.

Review is for the Service Department...

A few months ago, I recently leased a 2020 Explorer ST from another Ford dealership. I currently live in Lake Forest, and the dealership I leased it from is in Orange (closed to where I used to live).

Since Santa Margarita Ford is my nearest dealership, I decided to take my SUV over here since it seems they're not busy (just calling in for an appointment, I can drop it off whenever).

I visited this dealership 3 times:
1st - Had a hyperblinking issue on the left turn signal that bothered me ($60k for a brand new car having this issue, and wanted to get it corrected). Please note this issue was not resolved by SM Ford, and that I had to have my originating dealer resolve it for me (even though SM Ford knew of the problem, but didn't want to help me since they're stating that it may not be covered under warranty).

2nd - Reverse camera intermittently is non-functional (displays blue screen). Please note that this issue is not currently resolved, but SM Ford technically ignored the problem and told me to wait for recall notice. I got my originating dealership involved, and they are ordering me a new reverse camera.

3rd - Broken seat panel caused by my second visit to SM Ford. During that visit, I noticed upon picking up my car that the power driver seat panel was slightly hanging. I briefly dismissed the issue because I thought the mechanic had to go under the seat (for reasons unknown) and forgot to clip the cover back on. Flash forward a week later when I cleaned my card, and discovered that a plastic clip was actually broken. Mentioned it to my Service Advisor and he misled me regarding the timeline (initially said the part will come in later that week, but upon my follow-up call today he's now stating the end of this month).

My overall experience at Santa Margarita Ford has been very negative, including the broken seat panel issue. I'm writing this review because I just got off the phone with SM Ford's Service Advisor (please note that I had to call because he hasn't been following up with me), and he now states that the part in question is on backorder and they should expect an update by the end of the month. Very non-confident on his part. By that point, I expressed my frustration to him, and even called him out on excuses he's been stringing me along to.

I just gave up at this point, and called my advisor at the Orange dealership regarding the broken seat issue that SM Ford caused, and he told me to bring it in and will take care of it for me...<//review>

Great job Santa Margarita Ford!

Car buying can be a fun but highly stressful process.The right dealership can make the most of the fun and minimize the stress.  That's exactly what happened at this Ford dealership.

The car was mainly for my wife, and her evaluation process is way different than mine.  Our sales rep, Blake, was awesome. He took both my wife's and my style into account when answering questions and explaining features. We never felt any pressure - we just good product knowledge and a friendly attitude.

Ultimately, we went back 2 to 3 times narrowing down and finalizing our decision.  Each time Blake was as patient as he was on our original visit. Blake then had to source out a few other dealerships to get a Focus with the exact options we wanted and he did so quickly and professionally.

I'd definitely recommend looking at Ford when you're considering a new car and Santa Margarita Ford is a great place to shop and buy!</Review>

<Text>I connected with the Santa Margarita Ford Internet Dept and asked them about the Ford Fusion Hybrid. I told Susan of the Internet Dept that I need to drive an hour to reach their dealership, and they should be honest about assessing trade-in value on my current vehicle.  Strangely when I got there, Susan never came out to greet me - I guessed too lazy to get off her chair to greet a customer who drove the distance to reach the dealership. As a contrast, at other Ford and Chevrolet dealerships, their internet manager/directors would personally come out to greet a customer just arriving -- I've been personally greeted by all the internet managers/directors at all the other Ford and Chevrolet dealerships.  I guessed customer satisfaction is not a motto at Santa Margarita Ford.   Instead, I was paired up with an older gentleman as my salesperson.  He was low-keyed and pretty easy to strike up a conversation.  This was a good salesperson.  We test drove a Fusion Hybrid that I picked out and everything went fine.  What went downhill is when they took my vehicle to their used car department for appraisal.  Since most customers carefully input the accessories and other stuff into the online Kelly Blue Book calculator and it would give you a printout of your trade-in value (within a tight range).  Armed with this Kelly Blue Book trade-in printout, I sat patiently for the trade-in assessment.  I was handed over to the sales manager for the trade-in negotiation and I knew this was going downhill fast.  The sales manager appraised my trade-in at almost over $4000 below the Kelly Blue Book trade-in value printout.  This is a total rip-off! And, the sales manager said that I would get similar low ball trade-in offer from other dealerships.  He said that I shouldn't trust the Kelly Blue Book trade-in value, and trust their used car department - Wow, I'm a professional and I don't need them to tell me this lie.  I WILL trust Kelly Blue Book and not trust their used car department.  With that, I left the dealership for a long drive home - wasted my time and fed a bunch of lies by the sales manager.  To prove Santa Margarita Ford wrong, I went to SouthBay Ford dealership (near LAX) and went through the selection of a new Ford Fusion Energi Plug-In and patiently waited for SouthBay Ford to assess the trade-in value of my vehicle.  Surprisingly, SouthBay Ford's assessment of my trade-in value matched the Kelly Blue Book trade-in printout that I was holding in my hand. This tells me that SouthBay Ford is truthful and transparent in its dealing with customers.  On the other hand, Santa Margarita Ford shouldn't be trusted by their customers.  Beware - you could lose thousands of dollars on your trade-in if you intend to purchase your next vehicle at Santa Margarita Ford.  If you don't believe, print out the Kelly Blue Book trade-in value from your home computer.  Take your trade-in vehicle to Santa Margarita Ford, and watch Santa Margarita miss your Kelly Blue Book trade-value by thousands of dollars.  If you still decide to go through with it, you just financed the ultimate Hawaii vacation for the Santa Margarita's sales manager, salesperson, and finance manager.  If it were me, I would rather take that Hawaii vacation myself instead of financing Hawaii vacations for others.< /Text></record></dataset><record>
